Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 27, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











22 Grand Prix Trials took place yesterday, granting their respective winners two byes as well as the much-appreciated Sleep-In Special. Interestingly, Death's Shadow only took down one of the Grand Prix Trials, despite being heralded as the best deck in the format. Abzan Company and Living End gain the most from *Amonkhet* and posted great results, while usual suspects such as Affinity, Boros Burn, and Abzan linger around.


Anyway, here is a summary of the winning archetypes.


* 3 Affinity
* 3 Living End
* 2 White-Green Tron
* 2 Boros Burn
* 2 Abzan Midrange
* 2 Abzan Company
* 1 Eight Moon
* 1 White-Blue Menfolk
* 1 Red-Green Titanshift
* 1 White-Red Control
* 1 Eldrazi Tron
* 1 Dredge
* 1 Grixis Shadow
* 1 Jeskai Control

Let's take a look at all 22 winning decklists! You'll discover that Modern remains as diverse and dynamic as ever!
